18F47Q83 Support Information

XC8-CC #pragma config Usage

#pragma config <setting>=<named value>
For example:
// External Oscillator Selection : EC (external clock) above 8 MHz
// Reset Oscillator Selection : EXTOSC operating per FEXTOSC bits (device manufacturing default)
#pragma config FEXTOSC = ECH, RSTOSC = EXTOSC
#pragma config <setting>=<literal constant>
For example:
// External Oscillator Selection : EC (external clock) above 8 MHz
// Reset Oscillator Selection : EXTOSC operating per FEXTOSC bits (device manufacturing default)
#pragma config FEXTOSC = 0x7, RSTOSC = 0x7
#pragma config <register>=<literal constant>
For example:
// External Oscillator Selection : EC (external clock) above 8 MHz
// Reset Oscillator Selection : EXTOSC operating per FEXTOSC bits (device manufacturing default)
#pragma config CONFIG1 = 0xFF
For example:
// IDLOC @ 0x200000
#pragma config IDLOC0 = 0x4095

PIC-AS config Usage

config "<setting>"="<named value>"
For example:
; External Oscillator Selection : EC (external clock) above 8 MHz
; Reset Oscillator Selection : EXTOSC operating per FEXTOSC bits (device manufacturing default)
config "FEXTOSC" = "ECH", "RSTOSC" = "EXTOSC"
config "<setting>"=<literal constant>
For example:
; External Oscillator Selection : EC (external clock) above 8 MHz
; Reset Oscillator Selection : EXTOSC operating per FEXTOSC bits (device manufacturing default)
config "FEXTOSC" = 0x7, "RSTOSC" = 0x7
config "<register>"=<literal constant>
For example:
; External Oscillator Selection : EC (external clock) above 8 MHz
; Reset Oscillator Selection : EXTOSC operating per FEXTOSC bits (device manufacturing default)
config "CONFIG1" = 0xFF
For example:
; IDLOC @ 0x200000
config "IDLOC0" = 0x4095

Configuration Registers & Settings

Register: CONFIG1 @ 0x300000
FEXTOSC External Oscillator Selection
LP LP (crystal oscillator) optimized for 32.768 kHz
XT XT (crystal oscillator) above 100 kHz, below 8 MHz
HS HS (crystal oscillator) above 8 MHz
OFF Oscillator not enabled
ECL EC (external clock) below 100 kHz
ECM EC (external clock) for 500 kHz to 8 MHz
ECH EC (external clock) above 8 MHz
RSTOSC Reset Oscillator Selection
HFINTOSC_64MHZ HFINTOSC with HFFRQ = 64 MHz and CDIV = 1:1
EXTOSC_4PLL EXTOSC with 4x PLL, with EXTOSC operating per FEXTOSC bits
SOSC Secondary Oscillator
LFINTOSC Low-Frequency Oscillator
HFINTOSC_1MHZ HFINTOSC with HFFRQ = 4 MHz and CDIV = 4:1
EXTOSC EXTOSC operating per FEXTOSC bits (device manufacturing default)
Register: CONFIG2 @ 0x300001
CLKOUTEN Clock out Enable bit
OFF CLKOUT function is disabled
ON CLKOUT function is enabled
PR1WAY PRLOCKED One-Way Set Enable bit
ON PRLOCKED bit can be cleared and set only once
OFF PRLOCKED bit can be set and cleared repeatedly
CSWEN Clock Switch Enable bit
OFF The NOSC and NDIV bits cannot be changed by user software
ON Writing to NOSC and NDIV is allowed
JTAGEN JTAG Enable bit
ON Enable JTAG Boundary Scan mode and pins
OFF Disable JTAG Boundary Scan mode, JTAG pins revert to user functions
FCMEN Fail-Safe Clock Monitor Enable bit
OFF Fail-Safe Clock Monitor disabled
ON Fail-Safe Clock Monitor enabled
FCMENP Fail-Safe Clock Monitor -Primary XTAL Enable bit
OFF FSCM timer will not set FSCMP bit or OSFIF interrupt on Primary XTAL failure
ON FSCM timer will set FSCMP bit and OSFIF interrupt on Primary XTAL failure
FCMENS Fail-Safe Clock Monitor -Secondary XTAL Enable bit
OFF FSCM timer will not set FSCMS bit or OSFIF interrupt on Secondary XTAL failure
ON FSCM timer will set FSCMS bit and OSFIF interrupt on Secondary XTAL failure
Register: CONFIG3 @ 0x300002
MCLRE MCLR Enable bit
EXTMCLR If LVP = 0, MCLR pin is MCLR; If LVP = 1, RE3 pin function is MCLR
INTMCLR If LVP = 0, MCLR pin function is port defined function; If LVP =1, RE3 pin fuction is MCLR
PWRTS Power-up timer selection bits
PWRT_OFF PWRT is disabled
PWRT_64 PWRT set at 64ms
PWRT_16 PWRT set at 16ms
PWRT_1 PWRT set at 1ms
MVECEN Multi-vector enable bit
ON Multi-vector enabled, Vector table used for interrupts
OFF Interrupt contoller does not use vector table to prioritze interrupts
IVT1WAY IVTLOCK bit One-way set enable bit
ON IVTLOCKED bit can be cleared and set only once
OFF IVTLOCKED bit can be cleared and set repeatedly
LPBOREN Low Power BOR Enable bit
OFF Low-Power BOR disabled
ON Low-Power BOR enabled
BOREN Brown-out Reset Enable bits
SBORDIS Brown-out Reset enabled , SBOREN bit is ignored
NOSLP Brown-out Reset enabled while running, disabled in Sleep; SBOREN is ignored
ON Brown-out Reset enabled according to SBOREN
OFF Brown-out Reset disabled
Register: CONFIG4 @ 0x300003
BORV Brown-out Reset Voltage Selection bits
VBOR_1P9 Brown-out Reset Voltage (VBOR) set to 1.9V
VBOR_2P45 Brown-out Reset Voltage (VBOR) set to 2.45V
VBOR_2P7 Brown-out Reset Voltage (VBOR) set to 2.7V
VBOR_2P85 Brown-out Reset Voltage (VBOR) set to 2.8V
ZCD ZCD Disable bit
OFF ZCD module is disabled. ZCD can be enabled by setting the ZCDSEN bit of ZCDCON
ON ZCD module is always enabled; ZCDMD and ZCDSEN bits are ignored
PPS1WAY PPSLOCK bit One-Way Set Enable bit
ON PPSLOCKED bit can be cleared and set only once; PPS registers remain locked after one clear/set cycle
OFF PPSLOCKED bit can be set and cleared repeatedly (subject to the unlock sequence)
STVREN Stack Full/Underflow Reset Enable bit
ON Stack full/underflow will cause Reset
OFF Stack full/underflow will not cause Reset
LVP Low Voltage Programming Enable bit
ON Low voltage programming enabled. MCLR/VPP pin function is MCLR. MCLRE configuration bit is ignored
OFF HV on MCLR/VPP must be used for programming
XINST Extended Instruction Set Enable bit
OFF Extended Instruction Set and Indexed Addressing Mode disabled
ON Extended Instruction Set and Indexed Addressing Mode enabled
Register: CONFIG5 @ 0x300004
WDTCPS WDT Period selection bits
WDTCPS_0 Divider ratio 1:32
WDTCPS_1 Divider ratio 1:64
WDTCPS_2 Divider ratio 1:128
WDTCPS_3 Divider ratio 1:256
WDTCPS_4 Divider ratio 1:512
WDTCPS_5 Divider ratio 1:1024
WDTCPS_6 Divider ratio 1:2048
WDTCPS_7 Divider ratio 1:4096
WDTCPS_8 Divider ratio 1:8192
WDTCPS_9 Divider ratio 1:16384
WDTCPS_10 Divider ratio 1:32768
WDTCPS_11 Divider ratio 1:65536
WDTCPS_12 Divider ratio 1:131072
WDTCPS_13 Divider ratio 1:262144
WDTCPS_14 Divider ratio 1:524299
WDTCPS_15 Divider ratio 1:1048576
WDTCPS_16 Divider ratio 1:2097152
WDTCPS_17 Divider ratio 1:4194304
WDTCPS_18 Divider ratio 1:8388608
WDTCPS_19 Divider ratio 1:32
WDTCPS_20 Divider ratio 1:32
WDTCPS_21 Divider ratio 1:32
WDTCPS_22 Divider ratio 1:32
WDTCPS_23 Divider ratio 1:32
WDTCPS_24 Divider ratio 1:32
WDTCPS_25 Divider ratio 1:32
WDTCPS_26 Divider ratio 1:32
WDTCPS_27 Divider ratio 1:32
WDTCPS_28 Divider ratio 1:32
WDTCPS_29 Divider ratio 1:32
WDTCPS_30 Divider ratio 1:32
WDTCPS_31 Divider ratio 1:65536; software control of WDTPS
WDTE WDT operating mode
OFF WDT Disabled; SWDTEN is ignored
SWDTEN WDT enabled/disabled by SWDTEN bit
NSLEEP WDT enabled while sleep=0, suspended when sleep=1; SWDTEN ignored
ON WDT enabled regardless of sleep; SWDTEN is ignored
Register: CONFIG6 @ 0x300005
WDTCWS WDT Window Select bits
WDTCWS_0 window delay = 87.5; no software control; keyed access required
WDTCWS_1 window delay = 75 percent of time; no software control; keyed access required
WDTCWS_2 window delay = 62.5 percent of time; no software control; keyed access required
WDTCWS_3 window delay = 50 percent of time; no software control; keyed access required
WDTCWS_4 window delay = 37.5 percent of time; no software control; keyed access required
WDTCWS_5 window delay = 25 percent of time; no software control; keyed access required
WDTCWS_6 window always open (100%); no software control; keyed access required
WDTCWS_7 window always open (100%); software control; keyed access not required
WDTCCS WDT input clock selector
LFINTOSC WDT reference clock is the 31.0 kHz LFINTOSC
MFINTOSC WDT reference clock is the 32kHz MFINTOSC output
SOSC WDT reference clock is SOSC
SC Software Control
Register: CONFIG7 @ 0x300006
BBSIZE Boot Block Size selection bits
BBSIZE_512 Boot Block size is 512 words
BBSIZE_1024 Boot Block size is 1024 words
BBSIZE_2048 Boot Block size is 2048 words
BBSIZE_4096 Boot Block size is 4096 words
BBSIZE_8192 Boot Block size is 8192 words
BBSIZE_16384 Boot Block size is 16384 words
BBSIZE_32768 Boot Block size is 32768 words
BBEN Boot Block enable bit
OFF Boot block disabled
ON Boot block enabled
SAFEN Storage Area Flash enable bit
OFF SAF disabled
ON SAF enabled
Register: CONFIG8 @ 0x300007
WRTB Boot Block Write Protection bit
OFF Boot Block not Write protected
ON Boot Block Write protected
WRTC Configuration Register Write Protection bit
OFF Configuration registers not Write protected
ON Configuration registers Write protected
WRTD Data EEPROM Write Protection bit
OFF Data EEPROM not Write protected
ON Data EEPROM Write protected
WRTSAF SAF Write protection bit
OFF SAF not Write Protected
ON SAF Write Protected
WRTAPP Application Block write protection bit
OFF Application Block not write protected
ON Application Block write protected
Register: CONFIG9 @ 0x300008
BOOTPINSEL CRC on boot output pin selection
RA4 CRC on boot output pin is RA4
RA2 CRC on boot output pin is RA2
RC4 CRC on boot output pin is RC4
RC5 CRC on boot output pin is RC5
BPEN CRC on boot output pin enable bit
OFF CRC on boot output pin disabled
ON CRC on boot output pin enabled, selected by BOOTPINSEL<1:0>
ODCON CRC on boot output pin open drain bit
OFF Pin drives both high-going and low-going signals
ON Pin drives only low-going signals
Register: CONFIG10 @ 0x300009
CP PFM and Data EEPROM Code Protection bit
OFF PFM and Data EEPROM code protection disabled
ON PFM and Data EEPROM code protection enabled
Register: CONFIG11 @ 0x30000A
BOOTSCEN CRC on boot scan enable for boot area
OFF CRC on boot will not include the boot area of program memory in its calculation
ON CRC on boot will include the boot area of program memory in its calculation
BOOTCOE CRC on boot Continue on Error for boot areas bit
HALT CRC on boot will stop device if error is detected in boot areas
CONTINUE CRC on boot will allow device to continue code execution regardless of error detection in boot areas
APPSCEN CRC on boot application code scan enable
OFF CRC on boot will not include the application area of program memory in its calculation
ON CRC on boot will include the application area of program memory in its calculation
SAFSCEN CRC on boot SAF area scan enable
OFF CRC on boot will not include the SAF area of program memory in its calculation
ON CRC on boot will include the SAF area of program memory in its calculation
DATASCEN CRC on boot Data EEPROM scan enable
OFF CRC on boot will not include data EEPROM in its calculation
ON CRC on boot will include data EEPROM in its calculation
CFGSCEN CRC on boot Config fuses scan enable
OFF CRC on boot will not include the configuration fuses in its calculation
ON CRC on boot will include the configuration fuses in its calculation
COE CRC on boot Continue on Error for non-boot areas bit
HALT CRC on boot will stop device if error is detected in non-boot areas
CONTINUE CRC on boot will allow device to continue code execution regardless of error detection in non-boot areas
BOOTPOR Boot on CRC Enable bit
OFF CRC on boot will not run
ON CRC on boot will run

Interrupt Sources

The following table enumerates the IRQ numbers for this device along with descriptions of the interrupt sources. Also shown are the corresponding symbols that can be used as an argument to irq() in the __interrupt() specifier and the macro names that can be used in C source.

For example: __interrupt() specifier usage. 
	void __interrupt(irq(SWINT)) isr0(void) { 
		// do stuff
	}
For example: macro usage. 
	void __interrupt(irq(default)) isr1(unsigned char irq) {
		switch (irq) {
			case IRQ_HLVD:
				// do HLVD Interrupt stuff
				break;
			case IRQ_OSF:
				// do Oscillator Failure Interrupt stuff
				break;
			case IRQ_CSW:
				// do Clock Switch Interrupt stuff
				break;
			default:
				// do any other stuff
				break;
		}
	}
